Rest Architecture

## 

<span key="db88f898f8a7424eb88a93ba9bf781e4"><span offset-key="db88f898f8a7424eb88a93ba9bf781e4:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="5a0cb5635d2f43e0b5ba43b0f81817ec"><span offset-key="5a0cb5635d2f43e0b5ba43b0f81817ec:0">Introduction</span></span>

<span key="5b5cd01a290042ffb5eee40a1f6da363"><span offset-key="5b5cd01a290042ffb5eee40a1f6da363:0">API Browser Quick Guide</span></span>

<span key="3b73a900c97d47948070a76be3557751">**It can make your life easier**<span offset-key="3b73a900c97d47948070a76be3557751:1"> if you use some kind of </span>**API browser application**<span offset-key="3b73a900c97d47948070a76be3557751:3"> to </span>**explore the API**<span offset-key="3b73a900c97d47948070a76be3557751:5"> when diving into this documentation.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="726eb27025574cb48518727f0f302ca8"><span offset-key="726eb27025574cb48518727f0f302ca8:0">We recommend to use the free </span></span><a href="http://www.getpostman.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2faf81c1c0840b4bee07c6b7837dcb5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="2d74ba9107ee4a0aa25e1cd68ab313d3"><span data-offset-key="2d74ba9107ee4a0aa25e1cd68ab313d3:0">Postman</span></span></span></a><span key="94512fe2b913443fa23f1255ec5aa9ac"><span offset-key="94512fe2b913443fa23f1255ec5aa9ac:0"> browser plugin.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="7a37b95620034afe997133a175c4816b"><span offset-key="7a37b95620034afe997133a175c4816b:0">For easy onboarding take a look at </span>**our**<span offset-key="7a37b95620034afe997133a175c4816b:2"> </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/exploring.html#exploring-api-postman-onboarding" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="94e9066b74cd4f4aa6b77c0e0e34082f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="948eca07953e4b2eb10d9646cf2a5885"><span data-offset-key="948eca07953e4b2eb10d9646cf2a5885:0">Explore the API using Postman</span></span></span></a><span key="6c73fa713c4d46969b75a7c29d65695c"><span offset-key="6c73fa713c4d46969b75a7c29d65695c:0"> </span>**Quick-Guide**<span offset-key="6c73fa713c4d46969b75a7c29d65695c:2">.</span></span>

<span key="f795a16d39a5434f844eefd4ae92fa44"><span offset-key="f795a16d39a5434f844eefd4ae92fa44:0">A hypermedia API provides an entry point to the API, which contains hyperlinks the clients can follow. Just like a human user of a regular website, who knows the initial URL of a website and then follows hyperlinks to navigate through the site. This has the advantage that the client only needs to understand how to detect and follow links. The URLs (apart from the inital entry point) and other details of the API can change without breaking the client.</span></span>

<span key="8ae415d1c9ad4d92b15434a7ef4da58e"><span offset-key="8ae415d1c9ad4d92b15434a7ef4da58e:0">The entry point to the Plone RESTful API is the portal root. The client can ask for a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-rest" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f9fbe3be2ff4d3da2da6b8c0e0dcfe4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="1009240205dc401d8dc3e295ae76c8c9"><span data-offset-key="1009240205dc401d8dc3e295ae76c8c9:0">REST</span></span></span></a><span key="126b3ec1e9b84138b7ba6e1d018ba3a8"><span offset-key="126b3ec1e9b84138b7ba6e1d018ba3a8:0"> API response by setting the </span>`'Accept'`<span offset-key="126b3ec1e9b84138b7ba6e1d018ba3a8:2"> HTTP header to </span>`'application/json'`<span offset-key="126b3ec1e9b84138b7ba6e1d018ba3a8:4">:</span></span>

<span key="b891cc94b0d241e791ad369a63c7c5ce"><span offset-key="b891cc94b0d241e791ad369a63c7c5ce:0">http</span></span>

<span key="e723bce35cd64617a18c8f0b1083daf7"><span offset-key="e723bce35cd64617a18c8f0b1083daf7:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="1c57f6d15c3741e2a7a5962bd156e67a"><span offset-key="1c57f6d15c3741e2a7a5962bd156e67a:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="88bf778481b54c68a6463fa7f125bef0"><span offset-key="88bf778481b54c68a6463fa7f125bef0:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="0e804f23221f4597ae8876bde61e42ec"><span offset-key="0e804f23221f4597ae8876bde61e42ec:0">GET /plone HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="5fa1391b4f814897a1db8ef22574bc85"><span offset-key="5fa1391b4f814897a1db8ef22574bc85:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="18469505e1f040509c60282578518378"><span offset-key="18469505e1f040509c60282578518378:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyIgc3R5bGU9InZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7" />

Copied!

<span key="ac4c71a582b247a480416b98395c4208"><span offset-key="ac4c71a582b247a480416b98395c4208:0">This uses so-called ‘content negotiation’</span></span>

> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="636df5ce1649413691efecb396fef3b2"><span offset-key="636df5ce1649413691efecb396fef3b2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/content-negotiation.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8f3cca818c7749d28699b23c849c3590" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="1ba52e98c93d44bdbce966ec764f5a02"><span data-offset-key="1ba52e98c93d44bdbce966ec764f5a02:0">More on Content Negotiation</span></span></span></a><span key="b20efa794faf47ddb48b0f5dc2f15679"><span offset-key="b20efa794faf47ddb48b0f5dc2f15679:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="7fb3de35f9a746288488cd9b088f61af"><span offset-key="7fb3de35f9a746288488cd9b088f61af:0">The server will then respond with the portal root in the JSON format:</span></span>

<span key="48ab57d987cd442380e3e39433870197">`@id`<span offset-key="48ab57d987cd442380e3e39433870197:1"> is a unique identifier for resources (IRIs). The </span>`@id`<span offset-key="48ab57d987cd442380e3e39433870197:3"> property can be used to navigate through the web API by following the links.</span></span>

<span key="de028427a3c64eb189cbd7af68e10b7a">`@type`<span offset-key="de028427a3c64eb189cbd7af68e10b7a:1"> sets the data type of a node or typed value</span></span>

<span key="551404dc725d45cb8574d6147e55801c">`items`<span offset-key="551404dc725d45cb8574d6147e55801c:1"> is a list that contains all objects within that resource.</span></span>

<span key="3e852c8d45c0430f8f743abcf6e9dfbd"><span offset-key="3e852c8d45c0430f8f743abcf6e9dfbd:0">A client application can “follow” the links (by calling the @id property) to other resources. This allows to build a losely coupled client that does not break if some of the URLs change, only the entry point of the entire API (in our case the portal root) needs to be known in advance.</span></span>

<span key="eb6bc662106644839f3eaa045626d5fa"><span offset-key="eb6bc662106644839f3eaa045626d5fa:0">Another example, this time showing a request and response for a document. Click on the buttons below to show the different syntaxes for the request.</span></span>

<span key="54ee448be058400c9b518efaa9f713d2"><span offset-key="54ee448be058400c9b518efaa9f713d2:0">http</span></span>

>     <span key="d19c3cb0c5a8424d8b1e81b66d862912"><span offset-key="d19c3cb0c5a8424d8b1e81b66d862912:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plone-content.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bf029485805d41db95b6ba7692ffca09" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="2b4d1fb7a8c04b6a931b15dc39f9acee"><span data-offset-key="2b4d1fb7a8c04b6a931b15dc39f9acee:0">Representation of all standard Plone contenttypes</span></span></span></a><span key="1fbf9286eda24c2688676f809cdfbabb"><span offset-key="1fbf9286eda24c2688676f809cdfbabb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="e05890bc9e0940958ccc60d5bace683f"><span offset-key="e05890bc9e0940958ccc60d5bace683f:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="e828d475835447cea05e2adb435ad66d"><span offset-key="e828d475835447cea05e2adb435ad66d:0">Explore the API using Postman</span></span>

<span key="085e529f31ec4c9ab2f6d98583104909"><span offset-key="085e529f31ec4c9ab2f6d98583104909:0">To discover the API interactively, using </span></span><a href="http://www.getpostman.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0fa6d2127c8a49c79f3e832d216f9c80" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="f82d1213f0924696892e837db31d7c24"><span data-offset-key="f82d1213f0924696892e837db31d7c24:0">Postman</span></span></span></a><span key="68d6d6494ecb4d76ab41a526950b7a66"><span offset-key="68d6d6494ecb4d76ab41a526950b7a66:0"> is recommended.</span></span>

<span key="63cf87f6022446ac94fe25141832f69a"><span offset-key="63cf87f6022446ac94fe25141832f69a:0">Note</span></span>

<span key="511497fb3171470ba1f4a8b3a69ca3ff"><span offset-key="511497fb3171470ba1f4a8b3a69ca3ff:0">The Chrome-Extension version of Postman is deprecated and it is recommended to use the native app available instead.</span></span>

## 

<span key="a2a638763ddd4c4cab7c896c6ed560cf"><span offset-key="a2a638763ddd4c4cab7c896c6ed560cf:0">Configuration</span></span>

<span key="f4cd9ea63efb4d1ea364380854b05cb8"><span offset-key="f4cd9ea63efb4d1ea364380854b05cb8:0">To easily follow links returned by request based on the API,</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d07d049b7c254038bb4d5dc3dd986ed3"><span offset-key="d07d049b7c254038bb4d5dc3dd986ed3:0">go to the menu under the wrench icon on the top right</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="cec17e3e5ab148a996cb7d2652b641c0"><span offset-key="cec17e3e5ab148a996cb7d2652b641c0:0">choose Settings</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="abf296089a3340c4a98e6de00ee57e5f"><span offset-key="abf296089a3340c4a98e6de00ee57e5f:0">activate the option Retain headers on clicking on links by selecting ON:</span></span>

<span key="b126407f766c4c79869c1752e43c731f"><span offset-key="b126407f766c4c79869c1752e43c731f:0">postman-retain-headers</span></span>

<span key="a6099155b3fd4354b0a51d2caeacb72b"><span offset-key="a6099155b3fd4354b0a51d2caeacb72b:0">This option makes sure, once a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-http-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5d8006d084374fdcb0850e43a8b5c88e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="5cb9bef5d35f4abbbe909fa2f4cc3b15"><span data-offset-key="5cb9bef5d35f4abbbe909fa2f4cc3b15:0">HTTP-Header</span></span></span></a><span key="2eb1af7d00e6456e83cdaf0805693ed0"><span offset-key="2eb1af7d00e6456e83cdaf0805693ed0:0"> is configured, it will be reused during following </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-requests" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="daa4c8f579fd45dd90e9296b83062ed0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="244cb3f786ab4c43af20bf777493565b"><span data-offset-key="244cb3f786ab4c43af20bf777493565b:0">requests</span></span></span></a><span key="1d0634abd9b24b28b8748ee6bb917ca4"><span offset-key="1d0634abd9b24b28b8748ee6bb917ca4:0"> , if these are initiated by clicking on links resulting from the initial </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-request" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5d7ffe3aa25d4cb6abf788e4436cc3ad" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="d6844867559b4389831748dce7aef159"><span data-offset-key="d6844867559b4389831748dce7aef159:0">request</span></span></span></a><span key="93b7d8764e594c4fbf64456880a90565"><span offset-key="93b7d8764e594c4fbf64456880a90565:0">. This way navigating the structure using the API becomes a snap.</span></span>

<span key="56e24f43166e4150bfdeb242efdbbaaa"><span offset-key="56e24f43166e4150bfdeb242efdbbaaa:0">The option Send anonymous usage data to Postman should be deactivated by setting to OFF.</span></span>

## 

<span key="adea2917a84e4a27b9138f577a2be391"><span offset-key="adea2917a84e4a27b9138f577a2be391:0">Usage</span></span>

<span key="398ac278f6334d5090944f5906151e99"><span offset-key="398ac278f6334d5090944f5906151e99:0">Choose the suitable </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-13" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="622671261cf54a86afbd685545a75627" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="d28fb4273bfa41b79494b2e968a39dcd"><span data-offset-key="d28fb4273bfa41b79494b2e968a39dcd:0">HTTP Verb</span></span></span></a><span key="2ff90ddb55514a6d857df135336d3326"><span offset-key="2ff90ddb55514a6d857df135336d3326:0"> to be used for your request. This can be selected using the </span></span><a href="http://www.getpostman.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0a621eaeb6394f36a5116b8a91fc1eeb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="a3c8bca30e3d48938c0b544c5ebd94ac"><span data-offset-key="a3c8bca30e3d48938c0b544c5ebd94ac:0">Postman</span></span></span></a><span key="631f8c15435a4e76ae65df9ab2fc1e2c"><span offset-key="631f8c15435a4e76ae65df9ab2fc1e2c:0"> HTTP Verb -> GET drop-down menu.</span></span>

<span key="3f34233921cd458285a4f7a2a381aafa"><span offset-key="3f34233921cd458285a4f7a2a381aafa:0">Enter the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-object-url" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9c56eab7ff3e4dee9ebe0fef53d49c1b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="fb074b9b8a2d44b0be2d52570da91b78"><span data-offset-key="fb074b9b8a2d44b0be2d52570da91b78:0">Object URL</span></span></span></a><span key="fd0b5882d03547a9a0be5c8eaef26091"><span offset-key="fd0b5882d03547a9a0be5c8eaef26091:0"> of the object that should be the target of a request into the URL field right to the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-13" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f25b0324f044a3a8bf7a95c606729cf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="4f8d1a11069a437e9d2b2e8ba1ed35f3"><span data-offset-key="4f8d1a11069a437e9d2b2e8ba1ed35f3:0">HTTP Verb</span></span></span></a><span key="9d39ab34a7334f3585f522c21ead164e"><span offset-key="9d39ab34a7334f3585f522c21ead164e:0">:</span></span>

<span key="41773611d07e46a89f050b91804b8d83"><span offset-key="41773611d07e46a89f050b91804b8d83:0">postman-request</span></span>

<span key="b5f0b298e39f4b00a826c3bd62aad7c6"><span offset-key="b5f0b298e39f4b00a826c3bd62aad7c6:0">Now set the appropriate HTTP headers.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="0669bb4f6d954bdf901f8635b87aaa77"><span offset-key="0669bb4f6d954bdf901f8635b87aaa77:0">The </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-authorization-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="62a87bda009741f7b29d13fe3d8d0282" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="0b74793e49b9448bada58ed7485839d0"><span data-offset-key="0b74793e49b9448bada58ed7485839d0:0">Authorization Header</span></span></span></a><span key="8e1cd2969c524b2eb2ffad94cdb8b010"><span offset-key="8e1cd2969c524b2eb2ffad94cdb8b010:0"> for the authentication related to the right user</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7b6a23dac6784390800fd9f14cf6ae92"><span offset-key="7b6a23dac6784390800fd9f14cf6ae92:0">The </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-accept-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="008416436a5f4e098ca2a1864a4cebf3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="b012f9aed359488cb3b7694548e8232f"><span data-offset-key="b012f9aed359488cb3b7694548e8232f:0">Accept Header</span></span></span></a><span key="0189ed23e87e42149cba6b2ba5db56c6"><span offset-key="0189ed23e87e42149cba6b2ba5db56c6:0"> to initiate the right behaviour by the API related to this </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-request" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="21b3556f542248a1a565be476515f87e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="31b87b8f1d5147049155634a88358ad6"><span data-offset-key="31b87b8f1d5147049155634a88358ad6:0">Request</span></span></span></a><span key="5f8ed8c13528403688e1b581771e0b73"><span offset-key="5f8ed8c13528403688e1b581771e0b73:0">.</span></span>

<span key="606e6aaf5da74c68bf7bd57917f48949"><span offset-key="606e6aaf5da74c68bf7bd57917f48949:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0e299cd790bd40878cbe9c76c1e69d08"><span offset-key="0e299cd790bd40878cbe9c76c1e69d08:0">To set the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-authorization-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c4686ce1bbaf444dbaa126459ce5de7d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="6f04107d35bc43c8b64e6b83efe2ff26"><span data-offset-key="6f04107d35bc43c8b64e6b83efe2ff26:0">Authorization Header</span></span></span></a><span key="dc8d7e17750d435da9246bc9340da66c"><span offset-key="dc8d7e17750d435da9246bc9340da66c:0">, there is a reserved tab, that is responsible to generate the final </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="10a68202bf984d88998ffdf397eb0692" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="0997985bc27445059f5845505d8ad1f4"><span data-offset-key="0997985bc27445059f5845505d8ad1f4:0">Header</span></span></span></a><span key="2a644502cdf04d91aafb8c60748473c7"><span offset-key="2a644502cdf04d91aafb8c60748473c7:0"> based on the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-authentication-method" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b2be1890202045e68e6b9ae616b48426" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="62a2d45d770f490a9a818953e7c72447"><span data-offset-key="62a2d45d770f490a9a818953e7c72447:0">authentication method</span></span></span></a><span key="e22886ba9e824ddda1c643d12ebcd016"><span offset-key="e22886ba9e824ddda1c643d12ebcd016:0"> and username + password.</span></span>

<span key="157dc1351dd64ebfa5cb8a855f2d584c"><span offset-key="157dc1351dd64ebfa5cb8a855f2d584c:0">You have to select</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="985b53b8a16c430abdb030743b072c85"><span offset-key="985b53b8a16c430abdb030743b072c85:0">in the drop-down menu Basic Auth -> the term </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-basic-auth" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1176b2e0b3a2485bb64a1d378e734847" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="3246661c09054c6fa3e4744381ea1c33"><span data-offset-key="3246661c09054c6fa3e4744381ea1c33:0">Basic Auth</span></span></span></a><span key="1d143276bd144f0aa8a8ec5b8eff6e14"><span offset-key="1d143276bd144f0aa8a8ec5b8eff6e14:0"> as the authentication method</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7e3c9c4d451d41dc8035369a01bc91ec"><span offset-key="7e3c9c4d451d41dc8035369a01bc91ec:0">A valid existing user with appropriate permissions</span></span>

<span key="9f2b55d288974759ae4000aab25c4d3b"><span offset-key="9f2b55d288974759ae4000aab25c4d3b:0">After providing these parameters you can create the resulting </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-authorization-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="848883672b50461a8219e7f5606ca5b3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="4f6b3680b15a49b896d990eca374df0a"><span data-offset-key="4f6b3680b15a49b896d990eca374df0a:0">Authorization Header</span></span></span></a><span key="406eee7b5aae485f9de9d4f1cd5c4dc8"><span offset-key="406eee7b5aae485f9de9d4f1cd5c4dc8:0"> and insert it into the prepared request by clicking on Preview Request.</span></span>

<span key="dc5831594dcf491490f3df51e6f36574"><span offset-key="dc5831594dcf491490f3df51e6f36574:0">postman-basic-auth</span></span>

<span key="ea0c9fe3c78f4590bd422cd81b00429d"><span offset-key="ea0c9fe3c78f4590bd422cd81b00429d:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0bb7e3d1c0a44df0878943c524306085"><span offset-key="0bb7e3d1c0a44df0878943c524306085:0">Under the Headers tab you now need to insert in the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-accept-header" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b0ee2f306d5543d8962ff477fcaffd5c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="f8222f83f8624fe18bd741d2cd89f489"><span data-offset-key="f8222f83f8624fe18bd741d2cd89f489:0">Accept Header</span></span></span></a><span key="4c38d144268c49849fef52ac5031a767"><span offset-key="4c38d144268c49849fef52ac5031a767:0"> application/json\` header as well:</span></span>

<span key="5abc8d74aa604c0aa15f2ee0f9ef0fd9"><span offset-key="5abc8d74aa604c0aa15f2ee0f9ef0fd9:0">postman-headers</span></span>

<span key="7bd7a5a743cd4030bd962c50ab9e7528"><span offset-key="7bd7a5a743cd4030bd962c50ab9e7528:0">The request is now ready and can be send by clicking on Send button.</span></span>

<span key="836b51dd789f4b7692c5b075e223cd55"><span offset-key="836b51dd789f4b7692c5b075e223cd55:0">The </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-response" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5226095e7c734174a80c3c37c874a102" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="f72787603c5d4a3b9631bdbbe6c33b9d"><span data-offset-key="f72787603c5d4a3b9631bdbbe6c33b9d:0">Response</span></span></span></a><span key="500ce66878644cceaac070d7788adf09"><span offset-key="500ce66878644cceaac070d7788adf09:0"> of the server is now displayed below the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/glossary.html#term-request" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0104d2ee6aac4dc7a0743fdf2665b720" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="2d498db1da23470eb20cd95bec545ca6"><span data-offset-key="2d498db1da23470eb20cd95bec545ca6:0">Request</span></span></span></a><span key="76a68d06926d49dcbd3042b98687d68e"><span offset-key="76a68d06926d49dcbd3042b98687d68e:0">. You can easily follow the links on the </span>`@id`<span offset-key="76a68d06926d49dcbd3042b98687d68e:2"> attributes by clicking on them. For every link </span></span><a href="http://www.getpostman.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e2e0e6a60a244aabd95721232499012" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="937e0e5d823c4326a66daaa60c45f8e2"><span data-offset-key="937e0e5d823c4326a66daaa60c45f8e2:0">Postman</span></span></span></a><span key="9061b2799db44830ad212bf94033ef2a"><span offset-key="9061b2799db44830ad212bf94033ef2a:0"> has prepared another request sharing the same headers that can be send again by licking on the Send button.</span></span>

<span key="6fb81ba592b643c990af3af07e12c3f8"><span offset-key="6fb81ba592b643c990af3af07e12c3f8:0">postman-response</span></span>

<span key="b61c0f74ba4046aaa4b8025ccfad4967"><span offset-key="b61c0f74ba4046aaa4b8025ccfad4967:0">Conclusion</span></span>

<span key="3e2de4dc09da4d41973b4a8c420d283a"><span offset-key="3e2de4dc09da4d41973b4a8c420d283a:0">You can now explore the whole stucture of your application easily via the API using </span>*GET*<span offset-key="3e2de4dc09da4d41973b4a8c420d283a:2"> requests.</span></span>

<span key="ba6fe8500a3b420ea39e32222f7cdbed"><span offset-key="ba6fe8500a3b420ea39e32222f7cdbed:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="9ac4b64f332643e9a9d64c29bc94a5fd"><span offset-key="9ac4b64f332643e9a9d64c29bc94a5fd:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="b62fe11869854cdb9ffc1d605a5ed720"><span offset-key="b62fe11869854cdb9ffc1d605a5ed720:0">Content Manipulation</span></span>

<span key="2b979b5172844e2bba8257136f39ce38"><span offset-key="2b979b5172844e2bba8257136f39ce38:0">plone.restapi does not only expose content objects via a RESTful API. The API consumer can create, read, update, and delete a content object. Those operations can be mapped to the HTTP verbs POST (Create), GET (Read), PUT (Update) and DELETE (Delete).</span></span>

<span key="723f036fa13c4a6492514685351f4cdd"><span offset-key="723f036fa13c4a6492514685351f4cdd:0">Manipulating resources across the network by using HTTP as an application protocol is one of core principles of the REST architectural pattern. This allows us to interact with a specific resource in a standardized way:</span></span>

Verb

URL

Action

<span key="64915171ff254240a7425334e3208ecf"><span offset-key="64915171ff254240a7425334e3208ecf:0">POST</span></span>

<span key="9ca58951aea441b39351fab9594b900c"><span offset-key="9ca58951aea441b39351fab9594b900c:0">/folder</span></span>

<span key="b25fa390c5544af298ce7f44efc27ec2"><span offset-key="b25fa390c5544af298ce7f44efc27ec2:0">Creates a new document within the folder</span></span>

<span key="6bdd1041f7d84e729355a1f34e767dad"><span offset-key="6bdd1041f7d84e729355a1f34e767dad:0">GET</span></span>

<span key="802f4a4416b648c39b22663088a8518e"><span offset-key="802f4a4416b648c39b22663088a8518e:0">/folder/{document-id}</span></span>

<span key="3fa51d7bf7584448821f4d544508a874"><span offset-key="3fa51d7bf7584448821f4d544508a874:0">Request the current state of the document</span></span>

<span key="b8263a7018c14d42b55326bbfcb6beef"><span offset-key="b8263a7018c14d42b55326bbfcb6beef:0">PATCH</span></span>

<span key="7b198953e39742cba0634716cae582d1"><span offset-key="7b198953e39742cba0634716cae582d1:0">/folder/{document-id}</span></span>

<span key="4568bdeed2aa48b6853ad162f252cf73"><span offset-key="4568bdeed2aa48b6853ad162f252cf73:0">Update the document details</span></span>

<span key="eb8755fb97554da78f5a5c3331358b89"><span offset-key="eb8755fb97554da78f5a5c3331358b89:0">DELETE</span></span>

<span key="d6cac73ae4f3435fabebacd3ea1d527d"><span offset-key="d6cac73ae4f3435fabebacd3ea1d527d:0">/folder/{document-id}</span></span>

<span key="3a04c5c271b34078a83e9726927663a0"><span offset-key="3a04c5c271b34078a83e9726927663a0:0">Remove the document</span></span>

## 

<span key="9463545a350f46f1963e76db508850c5"><span offset-key="9463545a350f46f1963e76db508850c5:0">Creating a Resource with POST</span></span>

<span key="0ef741b002fc48f6bb9a6bcc0f1dc59c"><span offset-key="0ef741b002fc48f6bb9a6bcc0f1dc59c:0">To create a new resource, we send a POST request to the resource container. If we want to create a new document within an existing folder, we send a POST request to that folder:</span></span>

<span key="46dcd1cecf3745929d13f4b93795c672"><span offset-key="46dcd1cecf3745929d13f4b93795c672:0">http</span></span>

<span key="6ab97fe28290474eb9f3bd0bf80f7349"><span offset-key="6ab97fe28290474eb9f3bd0bf80f7349:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="b6980de9ee9e429393670f84d53866ce"><span offset-key="b6980de9ee9e429393670f84d53866ce:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="1cfd3eaeeee0491f9380f1ae156dc770"><span offset-key="1cfd3eaeeee0491f9380f1ae156dc770:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="afcdca8d04e74991b2bd2be0a8bec825"><span offset-key="afcdca8d04e74991b2bd2be0a8bec825:0">POST /plone/folder HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="44bfdac85cbf4989af92846cfbf2a664"><span offset-key="44bfdac85cbf4989af92846cfbf2a664:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="329b0977a0e4419db8227d86728b4ba4"><span offset-key="329b0977a0e4419db8227d86728b4ba4:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

4

<span key="bfb32653e0e0425ab7bf2c209a3d01c3"><span offset-key="bfb32653e0e0425ab7bf2c209a3d01c3:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

5

<span key="5dd18b6376ed4255bc4eaee496df02d4"><span offset-key="5dd18b6376ed4255bc4eaee496df02d4:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="9e93dea8e5eb470d9d47e546009200f1"><span offset-key="9e93dea8e5eb470d9d47e546009200f1:0">{</span></span>

7

<span key="e07ad268326c476ab13c4d23c557e17c"><span offset-key="e07ad268326c476ab13c4d23c557e17c:0"> "@type": "Document",</span></span>

8

<span key="1c7630ea8bbb4389b81fc5b5a11ae721"><span offset-key="1c7630ea8bbb4389b81fc5b5a11ae721:0"> "title": "My Document"</span></span>

9

<span key="87bb2adaa29e495baab99e8719633723"><span offset-key="87bb2adaa29e495baab99e8719633723:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="9c62d55d8c404c62b672a3c1edd5e17a"><span offset-key="9c62d55d8c404c62b672a3c1edd5e17a:0">By setting the ‘Accept’ header, we tell the server that we would like to receive the response in the ‘application/json’ representation format.</span></span>

<span key="2a89f3e0d1df4bfa9275df7db47c98de"><span offset-key="2a89f3e0d1df4bfa9275df7db47c98de:0">The ‘Content-Type’ header indicates that the body uses the ‘application/json’ format.</span></span>

<span key="d807458bceab4e8ca4c1ceea94486b1a"><span offset-key="d807458bceab4e8ca4c1ceea94486b1a:0">The request body contains the minimal necessary information needed to create a document (the type and the title). You could set other properties, like “description” here as well.</span></span>

<span key="82517b71c9c64387aa08c1343caa26fe"><span offset-key="82517b71c9c64387aa08c1343caa26fe:0">A special property during content creation is “UID”, as it requires the user to have the </span>*Manage Portal*<span offset-key="82517b71c9c64387aa08c1343caa26fe:2"> permission to set it. Without the permission, the request will fail as Unauthorized.</span></span>

### 

<span key="d0b583f2d52d4ed8bd8d8c935d98b378"><span offset-key="d0b583f2d52d4ed8bd8d8c935d98b378:0">Successful Response (201 Created)</span></span>

<span key="1be6724e5fc24a4285d043bdbc5b983d"><span offset-key="1be6724e5fc24a4285d043bdbc5b983d:0">If a resource has been created, the server responds with the </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-201-created" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="82847006c06a436584a2320d6e41fb27" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="11ce0e7cac344e07a1eca11b63333458"><span data-offset-key="11ce0e7cac344e07a1eca11b63333458:0">201 Created</span></span></span></a><span key="92abc92dae884171bc179ed7ce4c01f6"><span offset-key="92abc92dae884171bc179ed7ce4c01f6:0"> status code. The ‘Location’ header contains the URL of the newly created resource and the resource representation in the payload:</span></span>

1

<span key="1d4bfebac553486c97c52c9c86d29a94"><span offset-key="1d4bfebac553486c97c52c9c86d29a94:0">HTTP/1.1 201 Created</span></span>

2

<span key="c4473225eb73491da49351681b1f9b69"><span offset-key="c4473225eb73491da49351681b1f9b69:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

<span key="cbc7227cd87146a1aa416665b8add491"><span offset-key="cbc7227cd87146a1aa416665b8add491:0">Location: http://localhost:55001/plone/folder/my-document</span></span>

4

### 

<span key="388ff91b551e491d90500448a3851012"><span offset-key="388ff91b551e491d90500448a3851012:0">Unsuccessful Response (400 Bad Request)</span></span>

### 

<span key="5fdb47984eaf4d608d7cc0368fd19bef"><span offset-key="5fdb47984eaf4d608d7cc0368fd19bef:0">Unsuccessful Response (500 Internal Server Error)</span></span>

<span key="aa6ec979bc9446218aa9039c1ce9fc9b"><span offset-key="aa6ec979bc9446218aa9039c1ce9fc9b:0">If the server can not properly process a request, it responds with </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-500-internal-server-error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="88c7b7cfd7a4484f9eed40f2eb8c98df" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="e48c527d1db04a01a4f1138ca5a938f0"><span data-offset-key="e48c527d1db04a01a4f1138ca5a938f0:0">500 Internal Server Error</span></span></span></a><span key="e3919c28b8414d99b9bdda6f19325087"><span offset-key="e3919c28b8414d99b9bdda6f19325087:0">:</span></span>

### 

<span key="48e0520696084049bdd8e1d7ae712686"><span offset-key="48e0520696084049bdd8e1d7ae712686:0">Possible POST Responses</span></span>

<span key="57811d01df1d415499550dd40da858f1"><span offset-key="57811d01df1d415499550dd40da858f1:0">Possible server reponses for a POST request are:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="de9c2f37380e44efa7d7d7224c1eb31a"><span offset-key="de9c2f37380e44efa7d7d7224c1eb31a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-201-created" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d3dbdd61b8a44ace946d6efea8fd996e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="6a71869ac47d4cfcbedff289c0450175"><span data-offset-key="6a71869ac47d4cfcbedff289c0450175:0">201 Created</span></span></span></a><span key="4c4578b8bd234150a4b9d0168de70657"><span offset-key="4c4578b8bd234150a4b9d0168de70657:0"> (Resource has been created successfully)</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="55e99c89ff5d4aea9abd40b4b7213cb7"><span offset-key="55e99c89ff5d4aea9abd40b4b7213cb7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-400-bad-request" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="227a7d8b63dd447aa4d031e80c5520f2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="dd09f2ed972b4a08895bd759fddba3a9"><span data-offset-key="dd09f2ed972b4a08895bd759fddba3a9:0">400 Bad Request</span></span></span></a><span key="ab6f7b2e134e49618d2371a9f00e1d3f"><span offset-key="ab6f7b2e134e49618d2371a9f00e1d3f:0"> (malformed request to the service)</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ca0d214a21884d24b2b2543d6dda5c23"><span offset-key="ca0d214a21884d24b2b2543d6dda5c23:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-500-internal-server-error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="06c0f16b3d81460ca590d530ef0b2671" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="71ef2aed9dc34bbd8d3d137df0d9b507"><span data-offset-key="71ef2aed9dc34bbd8d3d137df0d9b507:0">500 Internal Server Error</span></span></span></a><span key="2332aeae7be541d8b611962c2f8ec4cd"><span offset-key="2332aeae7be541d8b611962c2f8ec4cd:0"> (server fault, can not recover internally)</span></span>

### 

<span key="58fe72e0370e44609216a2f89ffa8490"><span offset-key="58fe72e0370e44609216a2f89ffa8490:0">POST Implementation</span></span>

<span key="7f93059f5d64400a8abee91b18a60b79"><span offset-key="7f93059f5d64400a8abee91b18a60b79:0">A pseudo-code example of the POST implementation on the server:</span></span>

1

<span key="c885345b5f214b54b228954fcf94361e"><span offset-key="c885345b5f214b54b228954fcf94361e:0">try:</span></span>

2

<span key="489abc18bb2f41649ef0c75323b0c38d"><span offset-key="489abc18bb2f41649ef0c75323b0c38d:0"> order = createOrder()</span></span>

3

<span key="f645a8026b824c98bf0446151d934d81"><span offset-key="f645a8026b824c98bf0446151d934d81:0"> if order == None:</span></span>

4

<span key="a63f43ed06be4d87ac53d58a92362b1f"><span offset-key="a63f43ed06be4d87ac53d58a92362b1f:0"> # Bad Request</span></span>

5

<span key="9afbc5bc3cb14773ac085fcd580f7f3b"><span offset-key="9afbc5bc3cb14773ac085fcd580f7f3b:0"> response.setStatus(400)</span></span>

6

<span key="0f04ebedb2504f9081c2af7bf3496c04"><span offset-key="0f04ebedb2504f9081c2af7bf3496c04:0"> else:</span></span>

7

<span key="19bf03c53ccd4c47b5e3bba1eaaebf8a"><span offset-key="19bf03c53ccd4c47b5e3bba1eaaebf8a:0"> # Created</span></span>

8

<span key="51700142bc2f46df91fedd18bc6216af"><span offset-key="51700142bc2f46df91fedd18bc6216af:0">For folderish types, their childrens are automatically included in the response as </span>`items`<span offset-key="51700142bc2f46df91fedd18bc6216af:2">. To disable the inclusion, add the GET parameter </span>`include_items=false`<span offset-key="51700142bc2f46df91fedd18bc6216af:4"> to the URL.</span></span>

<span key="164f17356e2e456b9080da56bb65ac54"><span offset-key="164f17356e2e456b9080da56bb65ac54:0">By default only basic metadata is included. To include additional metadata, you can specify the names of the properties with the </span>`metadata_fields`<span offset-key="164f17356e2e456b9080da56bb65ac54:2"> parameter. See also </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/searching.html#retrieving-additional-metadata" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="195b74e6efb74b19953434abda585544" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="be4f38f9255f473f94b7b0fa588b9149"><span data-offset-key="be4f38f9255f473f94b7b0fa588b9149:0">Retrieving additional metadata</span></span></span></a><span key="54ceba87b476412d92248c631a9db473"><span offset-key="54ceba87b476412d92248c631a9db473:0">.</span></span>

<span key="02ab39a879a949cc88129db1968107c4"><span offset-key="02ab39a879a949cc88129db1968107c4:0">The following example additionaly retrieves the UID and Creator:</span></span>

<span key="1211ae74a7fe4e81acaa74661903872e"><span offset-key="1211ae74a7fe4e81acaa74661903872e:0">http</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="7e05b3de0c86497fa4f4ac94d06bfc81"><span offset-key="7e05b3de0c86497fa4f4ac94d06bfc81:0">Note</span></span>

<span key="dfe284b5b6cb4e2eaf1b0a15cd8e155b"><span offset-key="dfe284b5b6cb4e2eaf1b0a15cd8e155b:0">For folderish types, collections or search results, the results will be </span>**batched**<span offset-key="dfe284b5b6cb4e2eaf1b0a15cd8e155b:2"> if the size of the resultset exceeds the batch size. See </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/batching.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="58e6eb9c2e71478e8fcdae836c4d6f97" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="a8e5e99927a64c05a70ab9e148b8ee43"><span data-offset-key="a8e5e99927a64c05a70ab9e148b8ee43:0">Batching</span></span></span></a><span key="a6fd41dd813d4615ba74a46c28c32dde"><span offset-key="a6fd41dd813d4615ba74a46c28c32dde:0"> for more details on how to work with batched results.</span></span>

### 

<span key="b3953abd75d24abb897284a4d3c3dab7"><span offset-key="b3953abd75d24abb897284a4d3c3dab7:0">Unsuccessful response (404 Not Found)</span></span>

<span key="58ee4c1be9c344d6a976c061094f881d"><span offset-key="58ee4c1be9c344d6a976c061094f881d:0">If a resource could not be found, the server will respond with </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-404-not-found" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c94d06c5e7fe465289f345ce930212e3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="8fc7c0dcefd94d979754f2fbd2649029"><span data-offset-key="8fc7c0dcefd94d979754f2fbd2649029:0">404 Not Found</span></span></span></a><span key="eb381901ffc44ed4b3047f9d75ba5004"><span offset-key="eb381901ffc44ed4b3047f9d75ba5004:0">:</span></span>

1

<span key="5abdf0c0ea6145499d04b088da5d6ccb"><span offset-key="5abdf0c0ea6145499d04b088da5d6ccb:0">HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found</span></span>

2

<span key="e055311d470145238de8ef3367129ff3"><span offset-key="e055311d470145238de8ef3367129ff3:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="53d0288200934c49a0d44dc7862a34d0"><span offset-key="53d0288200934c49a0d44dc7862a34d0:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

4

<span key="f0d4366befda489ca02bb028e59e8a72"><span offset-key="f0d4366befda489ca02bb028e59e8a72:0">{</span></span>

5

<span key="d6165f681a334091aacc3af05da50135"><span offset-key="d6165f681a334091aacc3af05da50135:0"> 'error': 'NotFound'</span></span>

6

<span key="640a41a0bb5641d79287e3ff13efbf75"><span offset-key="640a41a0bb5641d79287e3ff13efbf75:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

### 

<span key="bb7cc28eec884a009925553f23812be6"><span offset-key="bb7cc28eec884a009925553f23812be6:0">GET Implementation</span></span>

<span key="679243782a7f483392a328c7cfd4235f"><span offset-key="679243782a7f483392a328c7cfd4235f:0">A pseudo-code example of the GET implementation on the server:</span></span>

1

<span key="744d53d4769f4e23b013ceddea81bda0"><span offset-key="744d53d4769f4e23b013ceddea81bda0:0">try:</span></span>

2

<span key="aff489d524704575818f0999b5cc57e7"><span offset-key="aff489d524704575818f0999b5cc57e7:0"> order = getOrder()</span></span>

3

<span key="bf3f4e5b4fbb448cb58f0d5b5621df2b"><span offset-key="bf3f4e5b4fbb448cb58f0d5b5621df2b:0"> if order == None:</span></span>

4

<span key="2e332fe4d2ce471d98e81090ab5d63c7"><span offset-key="2e332fe4d2ce471d98e81090ab5d63c7:0"> # Not Found</span></span>

5

<span key="7fa41d80451b4510a2b6aa6c6bb850a5"><span offset-key="7fa41d80451b4510a2b6aa6c6bb850a5:0"> response.setStatus(404)</span></span>

6

<span key="ba7eb8d6094e4e1e90a4b5e4def98dcc"><span offset-key="ba7eb8d6094e4e1e90a4b5e4def98dcc:0"> else:</span></span>

7

<span key="95d10f8a395542bab2876d59da2fb912"><span offset-key="95d10f8a395542bab2876d59da2fb912:0"> # OK</span></span>

8

<span key="7f10c88c58ef4ee3a0410010f7abdf0e"><span offset-key="7f10c88c58ef4ee3a0410010f7abdf0e:0"> response.setStatus(200)</span></span>

9

<span key="36ef8b20c80243338314987b308b5391"><span offset-key="36ef8b20c80243338314987b308b5391:0">except:</span></span>

10

<span key="41a8ea0aa964447e89200a50b1b5202e"><span offset-key="41a8ea0aa964447e89200a50b1b5202e:0"> # Internal Server Error</span></span>

11

<span key="db6256f58c21414486736526ae0318d7"><span offset-key="db6256f58c21414486736526ae0318d7:0"> response.setStatus(500)</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="15d2ff3510e24a6ba3caff0dd3167a3a"><span offset-key="15d2ff3510e24a6ba3caff0dd3167a3a:0">You can find implementation details in the </span></span><a href="https://github.com/plone/plone.restapi/blob/dde57b88e0f1b5f5e9f04e6a21865bc0dde55b1c/src/plone/restapi/services/content/add.py#L35-L61" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2a3ec9966e394251b63d81ded855bc09" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="6ae6d6f0c0c74820ad99deb34c5e5bc3"><span data-offset-key="6ae6d6f0c0c74820ad99deb34c5e5bc3:0">plone.restapi.services.content.add.FolderPost class</span></span></span></a><span key="b5e0c48e866f4a07b6e8732d8a4b3839"><span offset-key="b5e0c48e866f4a07b6e8732d8a4b3839:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="5db247b543d445f092dcd6c9737052bb"><span offset-key="5db247b543d445f092dcd6c9737052bb:0">GET Responses</span></span>

<span key="704c1a95ec694baf8a19101e6e69dba0"><span offset-key="704c1a95ec694baf8a19101e6e69dba0:0">Possible server reponses for a GET request are:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ecefd2c0f1b2446db0d04997c6f4a395"><span offset-key="ecefd2c0f1b2446db0d04997c6f4a395:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-200-ok" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="06b9aa5dc0f44856aa44ded92d78e031" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="80c80ed2fa434ae1a7ffd7b32b6691c0"><span data-offset-key="80c80ed2fa434ae1a7ffd7b32b6691c0:0">200 OK</span></span></span></a><span key="24203e95bbc541258779f99a471b2188"><span offset-key="24203e95bbc541258779f99a471b2188:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="3a59d662fe2147b7a99944d0ee4ddd60"><span offset-key="3a59d662fe2147b7a99944d0ee4ddd60:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-404-not-found" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e43ee2185fe4645ad5b80841c7b62a2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="9049315882af4cad8f7d55a0efba0563"><span data-offset-key="9049315882af4cad8f7d55a0efba0563:0">404 Not Found</span></span></span></a><span key="8edbc15697d74bbab6f26a0f4f0c8be2"><span offset-key="8edbc15697d74bbab6f26a0f4f0c8be2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9390bd9b5b624342a40191174618a4b2"><span offset-key="9390bd9b5b624342a40191174618a4b2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-500-internal-server-error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d312b23826b048309b7b17884895a7dc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="41aad6f4b87a40998d9c5984c248f20e"><span data-offset-key="41aad6f4b87a40998d9c5984c248f20e:0">500 Internal Server Error</span></span></span></a><span key="cb48a54375e2467ab11197351ae4c01d"><span offset-key="cb48a54375e2467ab11197351ae4c01d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="eae0f33b1ff4420abc2637fc26096ad4"><span offset-key="eae0f33b1ff4420abc2637fc26096ad4:0">Updating a Resource with PATCH</span></span>

<span key="ab4eb37b7f9e44ecaeb5ffa33f7fcc12"><span offset-key="ab4eb37b7f9e44ecaeb5ffa33f7fcc12:0">To update an existing resource we send a PATCH request to the server. PATCH allows to provide just a subset of the resource (the values you actually want to change).</span></span>

<span key="cc33535d0d4b4b18a65267ceaf72b1f1"><span offset-key="cc33535d0d4b4b18a65267ceaf72b1f1:0">If you send the value </span>`null`<span offset-key="cc33535d0d4b4b18a65267ceaf72b1f1:2"> for a field, the field’s content will be deleted and the </span>`missing_value`<span offset-key="cc33535d0d4b4b18a65267ceaf72b1f1:4"> defined for the field in the schema will be set. Note that this is not possible if the field is </span>`required`<span offset-key="cc33535d0d4b4b18a65267ceaf72b1f1:6">, and it only works for Dexterity types, not Archetypes:</span></span>

<span key="cf805ac5ceb0434ab5a377dc5ad19652"><span offset-key="cf805ac5ceb0434ab5a377dc5ad19652:0">http</span></span>

<span key="18a5b9e82c2640b8b0d61202800b9280"><span offset-key="18a5b9e82c2640b8b0d61202800b9280:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="3838977034a24cbb8e1765a6baadfb3c"><span offset-key="3838977034a24cbb8e1765a6baadfb3c:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="7aa4a1e36de44602a69b7d9eaeb2c1ab"><span offset-key="7aa4a1e36de44602a69b7d9eaeb2c1ab:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="3428bf6e3d9047e8b8c01bcf68dec1be"><span offset-key="3428bf6e3d9047e8b8c01bcf68dec1be:0">PATCH /plone/folder/my-document HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="4200fa5a4d794cb9b5bec34798c4c1e0"><span offset-key="4200fa5a4d794cb9b5bec34798c4c1e0:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="cd7ac3eb25914a98ac33de2feb7a2d6c"><span offset-key="cd7ac3eb25914a98ac33de2feb7a2d6c:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

4

<span key="fd8b77c2920745779761b3f99873832d"><span offset-key="fd8b77c2920745779761b3f99873832d:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

5

<span key="9a0d20eda8e2493fa7cc4cb4c029e98c"><span offset-key="9a0d20eda8e2493fa7cc4cb4c029e98c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="b11a14abf5594ec284216b8659b6eae0"><span offset-key="b11a14abf5594ec284216b8659b6eae0:0">{</span></span>

7

<span key="83171e4551524346b56a0994022b65c4"><span offset-key="83171e4551524346b56a0994022b65c4:0"> "title": "My New Document Title"</span></span>

8

<span key="be7543325d454dc3b227f619640da0bb"><span offset-key="be7543325d454dc3b227f619640da0bb:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

### 

<span key="c68a54060cd4449e9422ef27828415b8"><span offset-key="c68a54060cd4449e9422ef27828415b8:0">Successful Response (204 No Content)</span></span>

<span key="1c63f818701e4bcd9e0f5b9082ca3701"><span offset-key="1c63f818701e4bcd9e0f5b9082ca3701:0">A successful response to a PATCH request will be indicated by a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-204-no-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="54769ddcedbf48b9b4c90ae92259e271" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="2bb79db80e8c4fbc9cabb4704b3c8ae5"><span data-offset-key="2bb79db80e8c4fbc9cabb4704b3c8ae5:0">204 No Content</span></span></span></a><span key="80bd739d3c2c4930b389f563dcc8e476"><span offset-key="80bd739d3c2c4930b389f563dcc8e476:0"> response by default:</span></span>

1
