<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="dd0546087d73424f94c95709cd53ce0c"><span offset-key="dd0546087d73424f94c95709cd53ce0c:0">See for full specs the </span></span><a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc5789" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ac8c74bcafa34122b143f232f3312899" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="c0fa23c7c8484372a74a91b52e7199e3"><span data-offset-key="c0fa23c7c8484372a74a91b52e7199e3:0">RFC 5789: PATCH Method for HTTP</span></span></span></a><span key="8a380075ce7348febcfa6854c327dbce"><span offset-key="8a380075ce7348febcfa6854c327dbce:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="5296b2731c1042fdbdacf027560b589c"><span offset-key="5296b2731c1042fdbdacf027560b589c:0">Replacing a Resource with PUT</span></span>

<span key="985f25deb3274664a76b616bc9cebf6c"><span offset-key="985f25deb3274664a76b616bc9cebf6c:0">Note</span></span>

<span key="fd7120a2536f4d24ab7929c6a872463d"><span offset-key="fd7120a2536f4d24ab7929c6a872463d:0">PUT is not implemented yet.</span></span>

<span key="73331944025c42b59dd4cfdce4df148f"><span offset-key="73331944025c42b59dd4cfdce4df148f:0">To replace an existing resource we send a PUT request to the server:</span></span>

<span key="6b855948c3394f38a892810bdc77b8c2"><span offset-key="6b855948c3394f38a892810bdc77b8c2:0">TODO: Add example.</span></span>

<span key="e2d56abac5574d07878ccc1036fabadd"><span offset-key="e2d56abac5574d07878ccc1036fabadd:0">In accordance with the HTTP specification, a successful PUT will not create a new resource or produce a new URL.</span></span>

<span key="b0964f316410489f8d6e64e2ed8453fd"><span offset-key="b0964f316410489f8d6e64e2ed8453fd:0">PUT expects the entire resource representation to be supplied to the server, rather than just changes to the resource state. This is usually not a problem since the consumer application requested the resource representation before a PUT anyways.</span></span>

<span key="7802dfa16d4d4428836ea5257b386dd3"><span offset-key="7802dfa16d4d4428836ea5257b386dd3:0">When the PUT request is accepted and processed by the service, the consumer will receive a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-204-no-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a64fadcc653847369a0d3054b06dc53d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="ea7e0ec5849f452d834313468cbc7def"><span data-offset-key="ea7e0ec5849f452d834313468cbc7def:0">204 No Content</span></span></span></a><span key="03efd634c17a48ba97f03c27716b3a24"><span offset-key="03efd634c17a48ba97f03c27716b3a24:0"> response (</span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-200-ok" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f33862395f6422c9e2034eb0e061cf7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="8c3ac94dbe384eaf89a1ef7cb0925003"><span data-offset-key="8c3ac94dbe384eaf89a1ef7cb0925003:0">200 OK</span></span></span></a><span key="7169e2241aea41a18cc4975abb68599e"><span offset-key="7169e2241aea41a18cc4975abb68599e:0"> would be a valid alternative).</span></span>

### 

<span key="744377a1e6fa48218e2f1073b7ded910"><span offset-key="744377a1e6fa48218e2f1073b7ded910:0">Successful Update (204 No Content)</span></span>

<span key="1abff160a614409eb7a1a35af7b76b60"><span offset-key="1abff160a614409eb7a1a35af7b76b60:0">When a resource has been updated successfully, the server sends a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-204-no-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba689e84b4ad41d89ccbde9ac7dfa53f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="daf72d34a504497b8a45a6a598019922"><span data-offset-key="daf72d34a504497b8a45a6a598019922:0">204 No Content</span></span></span></a><span key="5384f78045ec41f687c0e1bab7048e53"><span offset-key="5384f78045ec41f687c0e1bab7048e53:0"> response:</span></span>

<span key="49a1aba17d7e4d31a7cb5b203b13da14"><span offset-key="49a1aba17d7e4d31a7cb5b203b13da14:0">TODO: Add example.</span></span>

### 

<span key="69317e5343874efbbe646242b1a04965"><span offset-key="69317e5343874efbbe646242b1a04965:0">Unsuccessful Update (409 Conflict)</span></span>

<span key="5486de60ca78443da7c04a05da3dffc4"><span offset-key="5486de60ca78443da7c04a05da3dffc4:0">Sometimes requests fail due to incompatible changes. The response body includes additional information about the problem.</span></span>

<span key="0720253af0ca418f8a7dfbf7d75ad9c8"><span offset-key="0720253af0ca418f8a7dfbf7d75ad9c8:0">TODO: Add example.</span></span>

### 

<span key="defe30cc31ff47fda0f902897eb40eda"><span offset-key="defe30cc31ff47fda0f902897eb40eda:0">PUT Implementation</span></span>

<span key="e56d65272c9a463eb9bb38ae8036386b"><span offset-key="e56d65272c9a463eb9bb38ae8036386b:0">A pseudo-code example of the PUT implementation on the server:</span></span>

1

<span key="1ddbf61d9dbc406bbb313523ef989e10"><span offset-key="1ddbf61d9dbc406bbb313523ef989e10:0">try:</span></span>

2

<span key="cfd859bdb9c248b4822348b4eb424f7c"><span offset-key="cfd859bdb9c248b4822348b4eb424f7c:0"> order = getOrder()</span></span>

3

<span key="4f725cb84a854205a897352e580498de"><span offset-key="4f725cb84a854205a897352e580498de:0"> if order:</span></span>

4

<span key="9a8ec2ae019149e0ae4eaef64f21f36a"><span offset-key="9a8ec2ae019149e0ae4eaef64f21f36a:0"> try:</span></span>

5

<span key="08f6fd0a61524e72a02daa4b7a95218b"><span offset-key="08f6fd0a61524e72a02daa4b7a95218b:0"> saveOrder()</span></span>

6

<span key="604aa096707142aa8b9002c362344a1c"><span offset-key="604aa096707142aa8b9002c362344a1c:0"> except conflict:</span></span>

7

<span key="481a5378ba28424baf255445469fd9a0"><span offset-key="481a5378ba28424baf255445469fd9a0:0"> response.setStatus(409)</span></span>

8

<span key="94d3f628513e4df2a6a11a6527d8ed3f"><span offset-key="94d3f628513e4df2a6a11a6527d8ed3f:0"> # OK</span></span>

9

<span key="4564fb21fc4149d481bb33e2721a1f6a"><span offset-key="4564fb21fc4149d481bb33e2721a1f6a:0"> response.setStatus(200)</span></span>

10

<span key="b3ae760329ba4abe9975ecdbdd48c19c"><span offset-key="b3ae760329ba4abe9975ecdbdd48c19c:0"> else:</span></span>

11

<span key="caf22d8e749d4ffc8797cc7bb6744a65"><span offset-key="caf22d8e749d4ffc8797cc7bb6744a65:0"> # Not Found</span></span>

12

<span key="356593abfc4e423f8ae84e2d37cdc192"><span offset-key="356593abfc4e423f8ae84e2d37cdc192:0"> response.setStatus(404)</span></span>

13

<span key="bfa66110f3b64549b98d565b3c9dbb01"><span offset-key="bfa66110f3b64549b98d565b3c9dbb01:0">except:</span></span>

14

<span key="c24f98fc039c41239f0d1877dc720d53"><span offset-key="c24f98fc039c41239f0d1877dc720d53:0"> # Internal Server Error</span></span>

15

<span key="4fb839f222f4400eb136193747eeaedf"><span offset-key="4fb839f222f4400eb136193747eeaedf:0"> response.setStatus(500)</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="44800e6758ad431c9510e0cd73d7d2c0"><span offset-key="44800e6758ad431c9510e0cd73d7d2c0:0">TODO: Link to the real implementation…</span></span>

### 

<span key="1faf9945b1e642c8ab349911f2b83c70"><span offset-key="1faf9945b1e642c8ab349911f2b83c70:0">PUT Responses</span></span>

<span key="69eb106993d241afa588ffd68c7abd3a"><span offset-key="69eb106993d241afa588ffd68c7abd3a:0">Possible server reponses for a PUT request are:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="fd07eb86c5a44a10af8025b35bf35ea8"><span offset-key="fd07eb86c5a44a10af8025b35bf35ea8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-200-ok" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0273d1aa267c4b2db6294661e9e375fa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="82335a5b8e0846dab35413473eff8918"><span data-offset-key="82335a5b8e0846dab35413473eff8918:0">200 OK</span></span></span></a><span key="0d44f096e50b4f07a2daaf5d0a8724e1"><span offset-key="0d44f096e50b4f07a2daaf5d0a8724e1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="1d4da4a954be4eac8e2d90f73870fb75"><span offset-key="1d4da4a954be4eac8e2d90f73870fb75:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-404-not-found" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b5f6ff7662e149e6b95f98d9acfb151c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="69b13b187f7147df9e6ee0f8dbb4fc32"><span data-offset-key="69b13b187f7147df9e6ee0f8dbb4fc32:0">404 Not Found</span></span></span></a><span key="8bc951f0d0884211b51a8d645c4c0586"><span offset-key="8bc951f0d0884211b51a8d645c4c0586:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="51f56beb1dc943078d8563461910459c"><span offset-key="51f56beb1dc943078d8563461910459c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-409-conflict" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="820aac7e808f4f7d89e6f9c4d5105f6c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="ca82f72bbdad4b3b8897d88bbf38fc99"><span data-offset-key="ca82f72bbdad4b3b8897d88bbf38fc99:0">409 Conflict</span></span></span></a><span key="f4c5575d7cae4a47842473805b15f131"><span offset-key="f4c5575d7cae4a47842473805b15f131:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="523593a1dae644cb81e827584203ddfc"><span offset-key="523593a1dae644cb81e827584203ddfc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-500-internal-server-error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2befd032e66d4745b1e97926d28b6295" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="2f65ab8055204527986f1fb5c9fcd0ee"><span data-offset-key="2f65ab8055204527986f1fb5c9fcd0ee:0">500 Internal Server Error</span></span></span></a><span key="2f8f030a17cd4c10b5cfc6eb4fbde4f9"><span offset-key="2f8f030a17cd4c10b5cfc6eb4fbde4f9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="c4f15b4749ba4f6c9f18bc1102525d19"><span offset-key="c4f15b4749ba4f6c9f18bc1102525d19:0">POST vs. PUT</span></span>

<span key="51aeaf64b40d4d33bfe2a4ce909f15c5"><span offset-key="51aeaf64b40d4d33bfe2a4ce909f15c5:0">Difference between POST and PUT:</span></span>

> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="a925c209cfbe443d9c96a5a1732b9d4c"><span offset-key="a925c209cfbe443d9c96a5a1732b9d4c:0">Use POST to create a resource identified by a service-generated URI</span></span>
>
> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="53039cf20233453ab99ce976f6039d13"><span offset-key="53039cf20233453ab99ce976f6039d13:0">Use POST to append a resource to a collection identified by a service-generated URI</span></span>
>
> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="6eeea6fb406f4913bd0bb156069a02f9"><span offset-key="6eeea6fb406f4913bd0bb156069a02f9:0">Use PUT to overwrite a resource</span></span>

<span key="fb4b8b75f4e24106ab0a08a05f9e3bc1"><span offset-key="fb4b8b75f4e24106ab0a08a05f9e3bc1:0">This follows </span></span><a href="https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-4.3.4" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a1ff9ff686144e2e8f49779ce463083e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="41c17261ef774e7aba1452086e91282a"><span data-offset-key="41c17261ef774e7aba1452086e91282a:0">RFC 7231: HTTP 1.1: PUT Method</span></span></span></a><span key="1b58f73de0bd426e90c20dd19ca266c3"><span offset-key="1b58f73de0bd426e90c20dd19ca266c3:0">.</span></span>

## 

<span key="a9cfcbe84e7242b8b9754cc41f09db79"><span offset-key="a9cfcbe84e7242b8b9754cc41f09db79:0">Removing a Resource with DELETE</span></span>

<span key="93bdc96faca0476d982579cf4beebde5"><span offset-key="93bdc96faca0476d982579cf4beebde5:0">We can delete an existing resource by sending a DELETE request:</span></span>

<span key="c5cc2f5ae0d244659ed483b475abdd96"><span offset-key="c5cc2f5ae0d244659ed483b475abdd96:0">http</span></span>

<span key="b3765ebd94444f87820501a2f0649b45"><span offset-key="b3765ebd94444f87820501a2f0649b45:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="08da46adda46426eae147fa6600c2122"><span offset-key="08da46adda46426eae147fa6600c2122:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="da1df614750244e6bda5249df6ebcc33"><span offset-key="da1df614750244e6bda5249df6ebcc33:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="7c531367723c4a17b140b2f7d0153698"><span offset-key="7c531367723c4a17b140b2f7d0153698:0">DELETE /plone/folder/my-document HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="a3942907258f47b29518998a1b5ee96a"><span offset-key="a3942907258f47b29518998a1b5ee96a:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="b32b25253923460e9220007ba16028c9"><span offset-key="b32b25253923460e9220007ba16028c9:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="f51b985acfa844f1bd92babbac211221"><span offset-key="f51b985acfa844f1bd92babbac211221:0">A successful response will be indicated by a </span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-204-no-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fbfeee051d4c46fe88675e12d85d89a3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="d44fd9720129404baa2aeea8b2662af1"><span data-offset-key="d44fd9720129404baa2aeea8b2662af1:0">204 No Content</span></span></span></a><span key="a2220083ba1e4711b3b113fcbd518843"><span offset-key="a2220083ba1e4711b3b113fcbd518843:0"> response:</span></span>

1

<span key="04f23b6bc9094df79e5ff7c6a9f97a91"><span offset-key="04f23b6bc9094df79e5ff7c6a9f97a91:0">HTTP/1.1 204 No Content</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

### 

<span key="33bacac3b3bd49288a0eb2025fcac927"><span offset-key="33bacac3b3bd49288a0eb2025fcac927:0">DELETE Implementation</span></span>

<span key="b789334f9e1746eb94d63188695ffa53"><span offset-key="b789334f9e1746eb94d63188695ffa53:0">A pseudo-code example of the DELETE implementation on the server:</span></span>

1

<span key="403323c8ddd64af0b2b687e9f7cd6a74"><span offset-key="403323c8ddd64af0b2b687e9f7cd6a74:0">try:</span></span>

2

<span key="658168ed849c48d1b5e454387b4e1a07"><span offset-key="658168ed849c48d1b5e454387b4e1a07:0"> order = getOrder()</span></span>

3

<span key="14c67e6471a8494e864181c490a93a1c"><span offset-key="14c67e6471a8494e864181c490a93a1c:0"> if order:</span></span>

4

<span key="a1244af0b52c45eeafd9f9dc489e67c9"><span offset-key="a1244af0b52c45eeafd9f9dc489e67c9:0"> if can\_delete(order):</span></span>

5

<span key="c656e1f5f3784203a5542ef907c96221"><span offset-key="c656e1f5f3784203a5542ef907c96221:0"> # No Content</span></span>

6

<span key="49d0bc9d715d4137a42c4d997b8621f9"><span offset-key="49d0bc9d715d4137a42c4d997b8621f9:0"> response.setStatus(204)</span></span>

7

<span key="f12f2916d31d4002bbd7d677fd6050cc"><span offset-key="f12f2916d31d4002bbd7d677fd6050cc:0"> else:</span></span>

8

<span key="ea74fa9fe8f14ffbba1846e9ac52d103"><span offset-key="ea74fa9fe8f14ffbba1846e9ac52d103:0"> # Not Allowed</span></span>

9

<span key="34b78167b0e34b3db1cb8b61dd273008"><span offset-key="34b78167b0e34b3db1cb8b61dd273008:0"> response.setStatus(405)</span></span>

10

<span key="15484ed87a9f4c87b9c305aa9ecd32ea"><span offset-key="15484ed87a9f4c87b9c305aa9ecd32ea:0"> else:</span></span>

11

<span key="ded606d876014c33bf10320dc29bf518"><span offset-key="ded606d876014c33bf10320dc29bf518:0"> # Not Found</span></span>

12

<span key="ccfe13d5e77144bba1da7f69320ce799"><span offset-key="ccfe13d5e77144bba1da7f69320ce799:0"> response.setStatus(404)</span></span>

13

<span key="b6cd31296b784a44bc0f7d732fa8c456"><span offset-key="b6cd31296b784a44bc0f7d732fa8c456:0">except:</span></span>

14

<span key="3a79839f35554ee881456e350152421a"><span offset-key="3a79839f35554ee881456e350152421a:0"> # Internal Server Error</span></span>

15

<span key="602243af6da14cfe8565c66cadb0af37"><span offset-key="602243af6da14cfe8565c66cadb0af37:0"> response.setStatus(500)</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="e0d7ee7c4726431ba28ac128d5cbd798"><span offset-key="e0d7ee7c4726431ba28ac128d5cbd798:0">DELETE Responses</span></span>

<span key="d70b2791280c46288f3ee8605a96b48b"><span offset-key="d70b2791280c46288f3ee8605a96b48b:0">Possible responses to a delete request are:</span></span>

> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="b6fe1c8450764d5a9132b994354e42b6"><span offset-key="b6fe1c8450764d5a9132b994354e42b6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-204-no-content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a21bd4e234614d7785e84c5ad6e36b71" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="51a0cea51adf4d31894402cc949d5917"><span data-offset-key="51a0cea51adf4d31894402cc949d5917:0">204 No Content</span></span></span></a><span key="9921533c850946e0856ca75cd4c5e775"><span offset-key="9921533c850946e0856ca75cd4c5e775:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>
>
> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="c45267a178814801b089f98abb7748fe"><span offset-key="c45267a178814801b089f98abb7748fe:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-404-not-found" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="15af769024454a3c957fcc625f8ff93c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="290c498954fc4559a83ca2fb1c8ef3a0"><span data-offset-key="290c498954fc4559a83ca2fb1c8ef3a0:0">404 Not Found</span></span></span></a><span key="a84d0e28f5c042188cbb8273396598aa"><span offset-key="a84d0e28f5c042188cbb8273396598aa:0"> (if the resource does not exist)</span></span>
>
> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="f5309767e0fd433bab70a92e8b2e9ec2"><span offset-key="f5309767e0fd433bab70a92e8b2e9ec2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-405-method-not-allowed" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="83a79183d9c046ada1ee2d460f2a0f1d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="003dec2fcaa14bb98a730c3ce36fa842"><span data-offset-key="003dec2fcaa14bb98a730c3ce36fa842:0">405 Method Not Allowed</span></span></span></a><span key="09e1792f0b894e47947fab9f1663c02c"><span offset-key="09e1792f0b894e47947fab9f1663c02c:0"> (if deleting the resource is not allowed)</span></span>
>
> -   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />
>
>     <span key="7c5c7dd856644879b9eef9eec67adbfc"><span offset-key="7c5c7dd856644879b9eef9eec67adbfc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://plonerestapi.readthedocs.io/en/latest/http-status-codes.html#term-500-internal-server-error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d91e20ddb19a49238832cf45600555f9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="22adfc1f10874047b7093a38d620a404"><span data-offset-key="22adfc1f10874047b7093a38d620a404:0">500 Internal Server Error</span></span></span></a><span key="fced7e34959349b5b64ad72e770c0dce"><span offset-key="fced7e34959349b5b64ad72e770c0dce:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="7803558e3b9b43be929fcb3f31e2572b"><span offset-key="7803558e3b9b43be929fcb3f31e2572b:0">Reordering sub resources</span></span>

<span key="f64c22d36db04fc981f19dbcdc76870a"><span offset-key="f64c22d36db04fc981f19dbcdc76870a:0">The resources contained within a resource can be reordered using the </span>*ordering*<span offset-key="f64c22d36db04fc981f19dbcdc76870a:2"> key using a PATCH request on the container.</span></span>

<span key="f8781ad5b8fa4cd3a597f2c1efb0aebc"><span offset-key="f8781ad5b8fa4cd3a597f2c1efb0aebc:0">Use the </span>*obj\_id*<span offset-key="f8781ad5b8fa4cd3a597f2c1efb0aebc:2"> subkey to specify which resource to reorder. The subkey </span>*delta*<span offset-key="f8781ad5b8fa4cd3a597f2c1efb0aebc:4"> can be ‘top’, ‘bottom’, or a negative or positive integer for moving up or down.</span></span>

<span key="9bdf666f974e403e98e135f91aa01f8d"><span offset-key="9bdf666f974e403e98e135f91aa01f8d:0">Reordering resources within a subset of resources can be done using the </span>*subset\_ids*<span offset-key="9bdf666f974e403e98e135f91aa01f8d:2"> subkey.</span></span>

<span key="63ba3b6e132b4f4d8c239631b935fbd2"><span offset-key="63ba3b6e132b4f4d8c239631b935fbd2:0">A response 400 BadRequest with a message ‘Client/server ordering mismatch’ will be returned if the value is not in the same order as serverside.</span></span>

<span key="00e2753fe2da4739bf35689405a166ff"><span offset-key="00e2753fe2da4739bf35689405a166ff:0">A response 400 BadRequest with a message ‘Content ordering is not supported by this resource’ will be returned if the container does not support ordering.</span></span>

<span key="544ec1c8acbf4071af1e8500fc5e1d5d"><span offset-key="544ec1c8acbf4071af1e8500fc5e1d5d:0">http</span></span>

<span key="747dfac86a1b4ad49ebd7f33f78e8bc8"><span offset-key="747dfac86a1b4ad49ebd7f33f78e8bc8:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="a7f016a7d3ac47d6a5aaf589cf131501"><span offset-key="a7f016a7d3ac47d6a5aaf589cf131501:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="101ebd5fd91e465d9982f6ce894bdaac"><span offset-key="101ebd5fd91e465d9982f6ce894bdaac:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="07897046503347e7bfe629b84bab232f"><span offset-key="07897046503347e7bfe629b84bab232f:0">PATCH /plone/folder/my-document HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="ed7bec89064a46b589edce42bb82f7ec"><span offset-key="ed7bec89064a46b589edce42bb82f7ec:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="f072899d00be4c28859fed9e2e46a049"><span offset-key="f072899d00be4c28859fed9e2e46a049:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

4

<span key="fc46630eb5cb4cf5b4ef7ce2bd9146d2"><span offset-key="fc46630eb5cb4cf5b4ef7ce2bd9146d2:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

5

<span key="a3130ee4ce9f4f858a6f289503f8aa55"><span offset-key="a3130ee4ce9f4f858a6f289503f8aa55:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="55649b6a481d45b28f111f3b97368327"><span offset-key="55649b6a481d45b28f111f3b97368327:0">{</span></span>

7

<span key="e1ae11ff14df4626a940bda9e9832e0f"><span offset-key="e1ae11ff14df4626a940bda9e9832e0f:0"> "ordering": {"obj\_id": "item\_3", "delta": "top", "subset\_ids": \["item\_1", "item\_3", "item5"\]}</span></span>

8

<span key="3246b9a6be7a4bfb84bf2fb871f89f54"><span offset-key="3246b9a6be7a4bfb84bf2fb871f89f54:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="b7e96ded368c4a0ea8ddd9ca7eb0ec48"><span offset-key="b7e96ded368c4a0ea8ddd9ca7eb0ec48:0">To rearrange all items in a folderish context use the </span>*sort*<span offset-key="b7e96ded368c4a0ea8ddd9ca7eb0ec48:2"> key.</span></span>

<span key="eb9b3e1b77a242ac945ba1611d60ac4f"><span offset-key="eb9b3e1b77a242ac945ba1611d60ac4f:0">The </span>*on*<span offset-key="eb9b3e1b77a242ac945ba1611d60ac4f:2"> subkey defines the catalog index to be sorted on. The </span>*order*<span offset-key="eb9b3e1b77a242ac945ba1611d60ac4f:4"> subkey indicates ‘ascending’ or ‘descending’ order of items.</span></span>

<span key="06179ce0878f40a8b0172752574ab393"><span offset-key="06179ce0878f40a8b0172752574ab393:0">A response 400 BadRequest with a message ‘Content ordering is not supported by this resource’ will be returned if the container does not support ordering.</span></span>

<span key="82a647a801dd4c7e9f9e6c8279f3c040"><span offset-key="82a647a801dd4c7e9f9e6c8279f3c040:0">http</span></span>

<span key="b873f1855cc9425e8612c0b4f3e4d7b1"><span offset-key="b873f1855cc9425e8612c0b4f3e4d7b1:0">curl</span></span>

<span key="901f02c5c7e94e658897d7beadd6b89f"><span offset-key="901f02c5c7e94e658897d7beadd6b89f:0">httpie</span></span>

<span key="05341b0fc93a42918c7b66f54494bc3f"><span offset-key="05341b0fc93a42918c7b66f54494bc3f:0">python-requests</span></span>

1

<span key="99f7b7a665f340e094207633c7d5aca6"><span offset-key="99f7b7a665f340e094207633c7d5aca6:0">PATCH /plone/folder HTTP/1.1</span></span>

2

<span key="ba984cc4abdd4017bef196bee8997614"><span offset-key="ba984cc4abdd4017bef196bee8997614:0">Accept: application/json</span></span>

3

<span key="7df7098113784d01aa6888d2a2df2f49"><span offset-key="7df7098113784d01aa6888d2a2df2f49:0">Authorization: Basic YWRtaW46c2VjcmV0</span></span>

4

<span key="5c443a92b5ae4d57bab1f9d03d2ec42b"><span offset-key="5c443a92b5ae4d57bab1f9d03d2ec42b:0">Content-Type: application/json</span></span>

5

<span key="facf1a419b5e4208960cd106cd7d599b"><span offset-key="facf1a419b5e4208960cd106cd7d599b:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="b9464e68725d42ffbc28f44f7fa5cea7"><span offset-key="b9464e68725d42ffbc28f44f7fa5cea7:0">{</span></span>

7

<span key="895733bf8ec14a1489d3854a38ff1e5b"><span offset-key="895733bf8ec14a1489d3854a38ff1e5b:0"> "sort": {"on": "modified", "order": "descending"}</span></span>

8

<span key="82a3fb35dd844635baf864a0a36a67f6"><span offset-key="82a3fb35dd844635baf864a0a36a67f6:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

# 

<span key="9952bb78b6e14910ba9088ce868ea707"><span offset-key="9952bb78b6e14910ba9088ce868ea707:0">Conventions</span></span>

## 

<span key="0b747666f9cc4fe39e2d3a52f2b15aa3"><span offset-key="0b747666f9cc4fe39e2d3a52f2b15aa3:0">Naming Convention for REST API Resources/Endpoints</span></span>

### 

<span key="1b2ea6d0b9d54eff9c68c63a3dd83518"><span offset-key="1b2ea6d0b9d54eff9c68c63a3dd83518:0">Nouns vs Verbs</span></span>

<span key="c4dafb8f3736445a8520f19012d20db9"><span offset-key="c4dafb8f3736445a8520f19012d20db9:0">Rule: Use nouns to represent resources.</span></span>

<span key="256d93c53a64449cb7ac954af8995f48"><span offset-key="256d93c53a64449cb7ac954af8995f48:0">Do:</span></span>

1

<span key="8fe621e0eb234860a8720f6818d03028"><span offset-key="8fe621e0eb234860a8720f6818d03028:0">/my-folder</span></span>

2

<span key="89b67c3859284c7bb8115a66c5dedbba"><span offset-key="89b67c3859284c7bb8115a66c5dedbba:0">/@registry</span></span>

3

<span key="4d47aa4bd8194edda50c7376485e531a"><span offset-key="4d47aa4bd8194edda50c7376485e531a:0">/@types</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d813731020304baa8ccc0541ebee2386"><span offset-key="d813731020304baa8ccc0541ebee2386:0">Don’t:</span></span>

1

<span key="01fab9ac04014876bd70f1eb45643fc0"><span offset-key="01fab9ac04014876bd70f1eb45643fc0:0">/createFolder</span></span>

2

<span key="492f19b26b8b443f91c32f906074b4f2"><span offset-key="492f19b26b8b443f91c32f906074b4f2:0">/deleteDocument</span></span>

3

<span key="3cc82df2d2c04badb83a45a42e9a0790"><span offset-key="3cc82df2d2c04badb83a45a42e9a0790:0">/updateEvent</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="5499ee61187a4e1db7873cce38b35386"><span offset-key="5499ee61187a4e1db7873cce38b35386:0">Reason:</span></span>

<span key="5659d26a62d8433fbc86275975782109"><span offset-key="5659d26a62d8433fbc86275975782109:0">RESTful URI should refer to a resource that is a thing (noun) instead of referring to an action (verb) because nouns have properties as verbs do not. The REST architectural principle uses HTTP verbs to interact with resources.</span></span>

<span key="48709c7df49e4d498cf11e2314ce7065"><span offset-key="48709c7df49e4d498cf11e2314ce7065:0">Though, there is an exception to that rule, verbs can be used for specific actions or calculations, .e.g.:</span></span>

1

<span key="a418be60c3174189b84316ad541611be"><span offset-key="a418be60c3174189b84316ad541611be:0">/login</span></span>

2

<span key="8c344f0a567546309ce6e17ba491f623"><span offset-key="8c344f0a567546309ce6e17ba491f623:0">/logout</span></span>

3

<span key="41774b9f37fd41868d5c248336b2e620"><span offset-key="41774b9f37fd41868d5c248336b2e620:0">/move-to</span></span>

4

<span key="41d35ea17c654d8c97b4165f157f8f81"><span offset-key="41d35ea17c654d8c97b4165f157f8f81:0">/reset-password</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

### 

<span key="914ee91f9a5940dfa80321b748d585f2"><span offset-key="914ee91f9a5940dfa80321b748d585f2:0">Singluar vs Plural</span></span>

<span key="d0beca6a01874c0e8875a7546337839a"><span offset-key="d0beca6a01874c0e8875a7546337839a:0">Rule: Use plural resources.</span></span>

<span key="6afa59b1d27c43158f9783625d8575f3"><span offset-key="6afa59b1d27c43158f9783625d8575f3:0">Do:</span></span>

1

<span key="814e44f3805f48db81ceffed4a650c36"><span offset-key="814e44f3805f48db81ceffed4a650c36:0">/users</span></span>

2

<span key="84b16f0837e34f4d8efdfc673fe7e470"><span offset-key="84b16f0837e34f4d8efdfc673fe7e470:0">/users/21</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="f28268af5dd14b4d8dcfe8d28e1c0548"><span offset-key="f28268af5dd14b4d8dcfe8d28e1c0548:0">Don’t:</span></span>

1

<span key="c2ac8f282a5f4c8a9cebffb4bb5236a2"><span offset-key="c2ac8f282a5f4c8a9cebffb4bb5236a2:0">/user</span></span>

2

<span key="7a0a53ff4f1b439ea3440002f6ae2058"><span offset-key="7a0a53ff4f1b439ea3440002f6ae2058:0">/user/21</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="74f2b663f82f450aae93d18eb7e4e8f2"><span offset-key="74f2b663f82f450aae93d18eb7e4e8f2:0">Reason:</span></span>

<span key="49607fde1e0f4dd591c2c2aeab8b2b1c"><span offset-key="49607fde1e0f4dd591c2c2aeab8b2b1c:0">If you use singular for a collection like resource (e.g. “/user” to retrieve a list of all users) it feels wrong. Mixing singular and plural is confusing (e.g. user “/users” for retrieving users and “/user/21” to retrieve a single user).</span></span>

### 

<span key="f8e0ce647d7846cda540221748f695b3"><span offset-key="f8e0ce647d7846cda540221748f695b3:0">Upper vs. Lowercase</span></span>

<span key="b71d8fe4d81e4a5f88bbe40e35d2fe27"><span offset-key="b71d8fe4d81e4a5f88bbe40e35d2fe27:0">Rule: Use lowercase letters in URIs.</span></span>

<span key="d2833b1c913b4117a5c686d20718aef8"><span offset-key="d2833b1c913b4117a5c686d20718aef8:0">Do:</span></span>

1

<span key="1e31f8417d294edc989cdcc4a9dd5eb8"><span offset-key="1e31f8417d294edc989cdcc4a9dd5eb8:0">http://example.com/my-folder/my-document</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="837f3f6e31284e5c9a03b802ea9f95be"><span offset-key="837f3f6e31284e5c9a03b802ea9f95be:0">Don’t:</span></span>

1

<span key="f28a7dc813c749b284dc180cefd9465a"><span offset-key="f28a7dc813c749b284dc180cefd9465a:0">http://example.com/My-Folder/My-Document</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="919f4422544241de8e7f8a6c8849fef6"><span offset-key="919f4422544241de8e7f8a6c8849fef6:0">Reason: RFC 3986 defines URIs as case-sensitive except for the scheme and host components. e.g.</span></span>

<span key="1addee4201584cf7aa507b55732e6399"><span offset-key="1addee4201584cf7aa507b55732e6399:0">Those two URIs are equivalent:</span></span>

1

<span key="8732691027394c8d9949732995867b16"><span offset-key="8732691027394c8d9949732995867b16:0">http://example.org/my-folder/my-document</span></span>

2

<span key="d2e0cae9c3db4c29b21b351863fce350"><span offset-key="d2e0cae9c3db4c29b21b351863fce350:0">HTTP://EXAMPLE.ORG/my-folder/my-document</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="0f27c554f15e41a49aced0a13a7ef09e"><span offset-key="0f27c554f15e41a49aced0a13a7ef09e:0">While this one is not equivalent to the two URIs above:</span></span>

1

<span key="90b061e1c57c45cc926ce093a2fdcf49"><span offset-key="90b061e1c57c45cc926ce093a2fdcf49:0">http://example.org/My-Folder/my-document</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="d54868304f0d4a36b0ae2bb5b8d28358"><span offset-key="d54868304f0d4a36b0ae2bb5b8d28358:0">To avoid confusion we always use lowercase letters in URIs.</span></span>

## 

<span key="7cdf9248e69f447f952a74bdfbbc39a9"><span offset-key="7cdf9248e69f447f952a74bdfbbc39a9:0">Naming Convention for attribute names in URIs</span></span>

<span key="766ab825e5084edb80318366a0a4afe4"><span offset-key="766ab825e5084edb80318366a0a4afe4:0">Rule: Use hyphens (spinal case) to improve readability of URIs.</span></span>

<span key="982caa3d32254ecaae5e8d5af410f4f2"><span offset-key="982caa3d32254ecaae5e8d5af410f4f2:0">Do:</span></span>

1

<span key="a7561fe383744577a0e69c1cd89db0dc"><span offset-key="a7561fe383744577a0e69c1cd89db0dc:0">/users/noam/reset-password</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="120a1a3560c443449db9c1d8db96d10f"><span offset-key="120a1a3560c443449db9c1d8db96d10f:0">Don’t:</span></span>

1

<span key="f970b2e46b96438583fb0b1a6e613d1f"><span offset-key="f970b2e46b96438583fb0b1a6e613d1f:0">/users/noam/resetPassword</span></span>

2

<span key="d2b43071422545d497ec417d89327d64"><span offset-key="d2b43071422545d497ec417d89327d64:0">/users/noam/ResetPassword</span></span>

3

<span key="f38ebdb2236648109ab032158f301ced"><span offset-key="f38ebdb2236648109ab032158f301ced:0">/users/noam/reset\_password</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="4392b0886f7b43c8a35c617bec8ae38b"><span offset-key="4392b0886f7b43c8a35c617bec8ae38b:0">Reason:</span></span>

<span key="250f5c41890c493db63d3f91735a0a9d"><span offset-key="250f5c41890c493db63d3f91735a0a9d:0">Spinal case is better to read and safer to use than camelCase (URLs are case sensitive (RFC3986)). Plone uses spinal case for URL creation (title “My page” becomes “my-page”) and mixed naming conventions in URLs would be confusing (e.g. “</span></span><a href="../../../../cdn-cgi/l/email-protection.html#90bffde9bdf6fffcf4f5e2bfb5a4a0e3f5fef4cfe5e2fccfe4ffcfe5e3f5e2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b2221ff1bdce47bfa15d8bd5d17d22c3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="13d605ced59048a198d36616580eb934"><span data-offset-key="13d605ced59048a198d36616580eb934:0">/my-folder/@send_url_to_user</span></span></span></a><span key="0ed28512e06448c3a60856d47a808a08"><span offset-key="0ed28512e06448c3a60856d47a808a08:0">”). Google recommends spinal-case in URLs for better SEO (</span></span><a href="https://support.google.com/webmasters/answer/76329" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5b05b7a78891428ab8d28f9764021346" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="31cafacbbe0e4cd7bdf6c78aa27a2803"><span data-offset-key="31cafacbbe0e4cd7bdf6c78aa27a2803:0">https://support.google.com/webmasters/answer/76329</span></span></span></a><span key="a112a3d7cb064b05a3673d50ba5331bf"><span offset-key="a112a3d7cb064b05a3673d50ba5331bf:0">).</span></span>

<span key="a52fd934a3c24fd9a206d20935189153"><span offset-key="a52fd934a3c24fd9a206d20935189153:0">Discussion:</span></span>

<span key="abb905182dbf435d83293c061fb54bfa"><span offset-key="abb905182dbf435d83293c061fb54bfa:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/plone/plone.restapi/issues/194" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="538a943d125c4fe599edc6583696d375" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-1856_259-1857-237__"><span data-key="1f323af035e849f9a971d2f8cd5bca84"><span data-offset-key="1f323af035e849f9a971d2f8cd5bca84:0">https://github.com/plone/plone.restapi/issues/194</span></span></span></a><span key="d399702258134d538e5a2a7447a6f2a8"><span offset-key="d399702258134d538e5a2a7447a6f2a8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="509019f465ed418798dc766def3f148c"><span offset-key="509019f465ed418798dc766def3f148c:0">Naming Convention for attribute names in response body</span></span>

<span key="b242edb3156044f38e31e1e69e6eb97d"><span offset-key="b242edb3156044f38e31e1e69e6eb97d:0">Rule: Use snake\_case to reflect Python best practices.</span></span>

<span key="e82d195bb9194b6b949c1e31fb9082f3"><span offset-key="e82d195bb9194b6b949c1e31fb9082f3:0">Do:</span></span>

1

<span key="eda6159ef4e543c18269bad809017456"><span offset-key="eda6159ef4e543c18269bad809017456:0">{</span></span>

2

<span key="c517694f86de435fbba19f12462dba61"><span offset-key="c517694f86de435fbba19f12462dba61:0"> translation\_of: ...</span></span>

3

<span key="c763cabec2bd493da958bb9c4ac88e1d"><span offset-key="c763cabec2bd493da958bb9c4ac88e1d:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d5ff29504f254ab5829224a2c3775e0b"><span offset-key="d5ff29504f254ab5829224a2c3775e0b:0">Don’t:</span></span>

1

<span key="3ce478db0975450cb78badaa00c0acc2"><span offset-key="3ce478db0975450cb78badaa00c0acc2:0">{</span></span>

2

<span key="1959ec455eed4c81b5c72792511f2e04"><span offset-key="1959ec455eed4c81b5c72792511f2e04:0"> translationOf: ...,</span></span>

3

<span key="a4482140c50a4625a3bf4dcdef7c63b3"><span offset-key="a4482140c50a4625a3bf4dcdef7c63b3:0"> TranslationOf: ...,</span></span>

4

<span key="4815f849fae1484194e7a7c871404e11"><span offset-key="4815f849fae1484194e7a7c871404e11:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xODYwXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d274e2b1b119458394a5490cfa550117"><span offset-key="d274e2b1b119458394a5490cfa550117:0">Reason:</span></span>

<span key="ac0931c8ed124074a9c7e127745323dd"><span offset-key="ac0931c8ed124074a9c7e127745323dd:0">We map over Python attributes 1:1 no matter if they are snake case (modern Python/Plone, Dexterity) of lowerCamelCase (Zope 2, Archetypes).</span></span>

## 

<span key="c2f4fbbea49f45c7abdd9cf431d35be0"><span offset-key="c2f4fbbea49f45c7abdd9cf431d35be0:0">Versioning</span></span>

<span key="c2d8ae9b82c34c4780b173ac33bd8b93"><span offset-key="c2d8ae9b82c34c4780b173ac33bd8b93:0">Versioning APIs does make a lot of sense for public API services. Especially if an API provider needs to ship different versions of the API at the same time. Though, Plone already has a way to version packages and it currently does not make sense for us to expose that information via the API. We will always just ship one version of the API at a time and we are usually in full control over the backend and the frontend.</span></span>

<a href="modules-grades-understanding-your-isa.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1awozwy r-14lw9ot r-190qawg r-z2wwpe r-rs99b7 r-4dj0k7 r-1loqt21 r-1quu1zo r-1ro0kt6 r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-nsbfu8 r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"></a>
